				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Tabulatura Nova, SSWV 102-158 (Scheidt, Samuel)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 parts, 57 pieces
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1624 - <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://opac.rism.info/metaopac/search?q=rism00000990057800&amp;db=251&amp;View=rism&amp;Language=en">Hamburg: Michael Hering</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Pieces&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Pieces</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantilenas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantilenas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Magnificats&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Magnificats</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="24 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Tabulatura Nova
</td></tr>
<tr>

<th>Composer

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>SSWV 102-158&#160;; RISM A/I: S 1352-1354
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">

</th>
<td>None <small>[<span class="icatassign">force assignment</span>]</small>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 parts, 57 pieces
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part I.
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. <i><a href="/wiki/Wir_gl%C3%A4uben_all%27_an_einen_Gott,_SSWV_102_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Wir gläuben all' an einen Gott, SSWV 102 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Wir gläuben all' an einen Gott, SSWV 102</a></i>
</dd><dd>2. <i><a href="/wiki/Fantasia_super_%27Jo_son_ferito_lasso%27,_SSWV_103_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Fantasia super 'Jo son ferito lasso', SSWV 103 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Fantasia super 'Jo son ferito lasso', SSWV 103</a></i>
</dd><dd>3. <i><a href="/wiki/Vater_unser_im_Himmelreich,_SSWV_104_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Vater unser im Himmelreich, SSWV 104 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Vater unser im Himmelreich, SSWV 104</a></i>
</dd><dd>4. <i><a href="/wiki/Fantasia_super_Ut._Re._Mi._Fa._Sol._La,_SSWV_105_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Fantasia super Ut. Re. Mi. Fa. Sol. La, SSWV 105 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Fantasia super Ut. Re. Mi. Fa. Sol. La, SSWV 105</a></i>
</dd><dd>5. <i><a href="/wiki/Warum_betr%C3%BCbst_du_dich,_mein_Herz,_SSWV_106_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Warum betrübst du dich, mein Herz, SSWV 106 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Warum betrübst du dich, mein Herz, SSWV 106</a></i>
</dd><dd>6. <i><a href="/wiki/Passamezzo,_SSWV_107_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Passamezzo, SSWV 107 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Passamezzo, SSWV 107</a></i>
</dd><dd>7. <i><a href="/wiki/Weh,_Windchen,_weh,_SSWV_108_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Weh, Windchen, weh, SSWV 108 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Weh, Windchen, weh, SSWV 108</a></i>
</dd><dd>8. Courante, SSWV 109
</dd><dd>9. Courante, SSWV 110
</dd><dd>10. Ach du feiner Reiter, SSWV 111
</dd><dd>11. Est ce Mars, SSWV 112
</dd><dd>12. <i><a href="/wiki/Da_Jesus_an_dem_Kreuze_Stund,_SSWV_113_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Da Jesus an dem Kreuze Stund, SSWV 113 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Da Jesus an dem Kreuze Stund, SSWV 113</a></i>
</dd><dd>13. Fantasia super 'Ich ruf' zur dir, Herr Jesu Christ', SSWV 114
</dd><dd><i>Canones aliquot.</i>
</dd><dd>14. Canon contrarius in 5. Cantio sacra. SSWV 115
</dd><dd>15. Canon contrarius in unisono. Cantio sacra. SSWV 116
</dd><dd>16. Canon contrarius in 5. Cantio sacra. SSWV 117
</dd><dd>17. Canon in 5. Cantio sacra. SSWV 118
</dd><dd>18. Canon super ut, re, mi, fa, sol, la. SSWV 119
</dd><dd>19. Canon ad decimam ad Basin sine pausis. Cantio sacra. SSWV 120
</dd><dd>20. Canon modo superiori ad decimam sine pausis. Cantio sacra. SSWV 121
</dd><dd>21. Canon in unisono. Magnificat 8. Toni. SSWV 122
</dd><dd>22. Canon in 5. Magnificat 8. Toni. SSWV 123
</dd><dd>23. Canon contrarius in 5. SSWV 124
</dd><dd>24. Canon in unisono. Hymnus O Lux. SSWV 125
</dd><dd>25. Canon in unisono. Cantio sacra. SSWV 126
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part II. 
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Fuga contraria. SSWV 127
</dd><dd>2. <i><a href="/wiki/Echo_ad_manuale_duplex,_forte_et_lene,_SSWV_128_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Echo ad manuale duplex, forte et lene, SSWV 128 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Echo ad manuale duplex, forte et lene, SSWV 128</a></i>
</dd><dd>3. Fuga. SSWV 129
</dd><dd>4. Cantio sacra: Herzlich lieb hab' ich dich, O Herr; 2 verse. SSWV 130
</dd><dd>5. Cantio sacra: Christ lag in Todesbanden; 5 verse. SSWV 131
</dd><dd>6. Fantasia. SSWV 132
</dd><dd>7. Hymnus: Christe, qui lux es et dies; 9 verse. SSWV 133
</dd><dd>8. <i><a href="/wiki/Cantilena_anglica_de_Fortuna,_SSWV_134_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Cantilena anglica de Fortuna, SSWV 134 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Cantilena anglica de Fortuna, SSWV 134</a></i>
</dd><dd>9. <i><a href="/wiki/Gelobet_seist_du,_Jesu_Christ,_SSWV_135_(Scheidt,_Samuel)" title="Gelobet seist du, Jesu Christ, SSWV 135 (Scheidt, Samuel)">Gelobet seist du, Jesu Christ, SSWV 135</a></i>
</dd><dd>10. Allemande: (Soll es sein)&#160;; 10 variations. SSWV 136
</dd><dd>11. Allemande: Also geht's, also steht's; 7 variations. SSWV 137
</dd><dd>12. Toccata super: In te, Domine, speravi. SSWV 138
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Part III. 
</li></ul>

</dd><dd>14. Hymnus de resurrectione Christi: Vita Sanctorum, decus Angelorum; 5 verse. SSWV 152
</dd><dd>15. Hymnus de Sancto Spiritu: Veni Creator Spiritus; 3 verse. SSWV 153
</dd><dd>16. Hymnus de sancta Trinitate: O Lux beata Trinitas; 7 verse. SSWV 154
</dd><dd>17. Credo in unum Deum. SSWV 155
</dd><dd>18. Psalmus sub communione: Jesus Christus unser Heiland; 6 verse. SSWV 156
